Some settings can be different in different languages.`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| [](#listingsconfpy-10)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-10"></span><span class="c1">`# ! A comment stating (translatable) is used to denote those.`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| [](#listingsconfpy-11)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-11"></span><span class="c1">`# ! There are two ways to specify a translatable setting:`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| [](#listingsconfpy-12)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-12"></span><span class="c1">`# ! (a) BLOG_TITLE = "My Blog"`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| [](#listingsconfpy-13)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-13"></span><span class="c1">`# ! (b) BLOG_TITLE = {"en": "My Blog", "es": "Mi Blog"}`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| [](#listingsconfpy-14)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-14"></span><span class="c1">`# ! Option (a) is used when you don't want that setting translated.`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| [](#listingsconfpy-15)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-15"></span><span class="c1">`# ! Option (b) is used for settings that are different in different languages.`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| [](#listingsconfpy-16)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-16"></span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| [](#listingsconfpy-17)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-17"></span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| [](#listingsconfpy-18)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-18"></span><span class="c1">`# Data about this site`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| [](#listingsconfpy-19)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-19"></span><span class="n">`BLOG_AUTHOR`</span>` `<span class="o">`=`</span>` `<span class="s2">`"Your Name"`</span>`  `<span class="c1">`# (translatable)`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| [](#listingsconfpy-20)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-20"></span><span class="n">`BLOG_TITLE`</span>` `<span class="o">`=`</span>` `<span class="s2">`"Demo Site"`</span>`  `<span class="c1">`# (translatable)`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| [](#listingsconfpy-21)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-21"></span><span class="c1">`# This is the main URL for your site. It will be used`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| [](#listingsconfpy-22)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-22"></span><span class="c1">`# in a prominent link. Don't forget the protocol (http/https)!`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| [](#listingsconfpy-23)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-23"></span><span class="n">`SITE_URL`</span>` `<span class="o">`=`</span>` `<span class="s2">`"https://example.com/"`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| [](#listingsconfpy-24)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-24"></span><span class="c1">`# This is the URL where Nikola's output will be deployed.`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| [](#listingsconfpy-25)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-25"></span><span class="c1">`# If not set, defaults to SITE_URL`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| [](#listingsconfpy-26)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-26"></span><span class="c1">`# BASE_URL = "https://example.com/"`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| [](#listingsconfpy-27)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-27"></span><span class="n">`BLOG_EMAIL`</span>` `<span class="o">`=`</span>` `<span class="s2">`"`<a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection" class="__cf_email__"                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            
                            data-cfemail="86ece9e3c6e2e3ebe9a8f5eff2e3"><code>[email protected]</code></a>`"`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| [](#listingsconfpy-28)   | <span id="listingsconfpy-28"></span><span class="n">`BLOG_DESCRIPTION`</span>` `<span class="o">`=`</span>` `<span class="s2">`"This is a demo site for Nikola."`</span>`  `<span class="c1">`# (translatable)`</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |

| [](#listingsconfpy-668)  | <span id="listingsconfpy-668"></span><span class="c1">`` # And then do a backup, or run `nikola ping` from the `ping` ``</span>` `                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
